< review>
Enjoyed my Italian meal here with a bunch of friends on a Sunday evening.  Not too busy.  Not too noisy.  But we did make a reservation beforehand.  Shared a bottle of Macchiavelli red wine.  Each had our own main course.  I had the Lasagnetta Del Borgo.  It was not what I expected.  Not the conventional layers of lasagna that you expect.  Instead it looked more like rolls of tagliatelle.  Taste was sufficiently fresh and rich.  Could do with a little more spice.  Portions decent.  Shared a tiramisu.  It was not fancy-looking but tasted good.  USD28 per pax for a group of 5.< /review>

I came to this place 2 times and both times I was treated really rudely by the server/owner there. She stated things like "In California the minimum percentage for the tip is 20%" and she personally checked for the tip value in there from everyone and complained about it to one of my friends that was paying less than he should, and that is just one of many examples of how people are rude in there. So, maybe buying the whole bottle would be better.

On the brightside though, the food is usually interesting. The lasagna and the gorgonzola pizza were really good, and the decoration of the place is amazing, very rustic and beautiful.</Text>

Carissimo Sergio. I miss this place and your craziness. I used to come with friends every Friday night 20 years ago. As young professionals, we would save up during the week and on Friday get that weekly shot of genuine Italian taste that reminded us of our European motherland. From 8pm till late. We ended up closing the restaurant with Sergio and staff every time, singing our hearts away with the help of fermented grapes. The best memories ever in this restaurant, including some epic birthdays. This restaurant has SOUL. Ain‚Äôt for everybody. Other reviews said it and confirmed to me it has not changed much. Yes the service may not be 100% following whatever standards. But it is still a true experience. To me it is like when you live in a small village in Italy: loud, sometimes crazy, slow sometimes and you‚Äôd better be acquainted to the locals. This tiny restaurant is an institution to me, and withstood the test of time. The food is truly authentic Italian, as well as the owner. I will be back there for sure this summer with family and friends very soon, travelling back to SF from old Europe. Get ready and prepare la pasta e la grappa grande Sergio!!!!! :)<//text>

<rating>4< /rating><response>None< /response>< text>
Super cheesy romantic Italian place, but food was awesome. You feel like you're in a really narrow Italian alleyway in the evening summer heat with the murals and decorations (and the lack of AC). Tables are covered in checkered cloth and wine glasses everywhere, but the food really makes this place great. Fresh pasta can be expected for sure, but don't skip out on the antipasto, which was a really large plate with a good variety of prochutto, olives, roasted garlic, artichoke hearts, and caprese (basil, fresh mozzarella, and heirloom tomatoes) . For mains, I did the meat lasganette and he had the penne alla puttenesca. Both were delicious and really flavorful. My lasagnette was made fresh and layered perfectly. The chef rolled out the pasta behind the counter and you could see him stretch it out. The sauces were delicious too. Bread was complementary and was great with the olive oil and balsamic vinegar. This might not be the cleanest place (glasses weren't completely shiny), but the food makes up for it.< /text>

<Review>After being disappointed is my daughters' previous dentist, I discovered this place through a Mommy & Me event in Santana Row and saw the stellar reviews and decided to give it a try.

My 5 year old and my almost 2 year old had a great experience today, as soon as you walk in the door the waiting room is very kid friendly and neither girl had time to be nervous because they were so excited to play with the toys! The receptionist was very friendly and very kid savvy. She smiled a lot and addressed both girls directly. My daughters were both very comfortable. It was a very short wait and then we went right into the exam room.

Also, the receptionist was very up front about what insurance would cover, percentages etc... Which I greatly appreciated because other dentists I have been to avoid mentioning any of that until you're quoted a crazy amount for treatment.

My husband and I decided ahead of time that we didn't want to do any unnecessary xrays and when I declined them there was no pressure and no repeated pushing, which was always experienced in the past.

The cleanings for both girls went really well, they watched Moana on the screen on the ceiling and were very comfortable. The hygienist was amazing! Both girls really liked her a lot. She was very patient and explained everything in detail as she did things. It really was a great experience.

When the dentist came to check their teeth after the cleaning both girls were comfortable. My 2 year old took a little coaxing to get back in the chair but the dentist was very patient and we were able to keep everything positive. They took a picture afterwards and both girls were happy! They also got stickers, a goody bag and a toy when they left. A little extra was a magnetic picture of them with the dentist which my girls loved. Also... No Cavities!!!

I would and will recommend this place to anyone looking for a very kid friendly dentist! I wish my dentist was this great! Thank you so much!!!<//Review>< Pics>

We arrived to get early seating for the band and the place was somewhat empty and quiet at about 5:30PM.  However by the time the band starting playing the place was absolutely packed ‚Äì I think even the owner was not expecting such a large crowd.   We haven‚Äôt been to this spot since it was Graffiti, so this was our first impression of this new Restaurant located in the attractive Waterfront district in Petaluma, CA.  So we started looking over the menu which was all new to us.  The waiter was very pleasant and eager to please and did a fantastic job serving us.  Things got super crazy with the crowd later in the evening and even when our waiter wasn‚Äôt available two other waiters popped by and took our drink orders for us.
The menu was great.  We started with an appetizer (called small plates on their menu) that was a special and not on the menu ‚Äì it was a hybrid between a Cheese Wonton and a Taquito and was a great starter with the spicy siracha aioli sauce and a fresh guacamole dip that also had a kick.  We wanted to try the Chicken Wings so we asked our waiter what his favorite was he recommended the Sticky Lemon-Pepper wings.  The appetizers were fresh and had great flavor and very satisfying for a starter.  We also started with a glass of wine and was pleased to learn their house Chardonnay was Hess.  It was served with a starting pour and a mini carafe ‚Äì it was a very generous pour if you took the carafe and poured into your glass topped of the glass very generously unlike their predecessor Graffiti who weighed and laser scanned their pours and charged you top dollar for them. Also we were pleasantly surprised that since we were there before 6 it was still their happy hour when we ordered them and it was $2 off their usual cost for a glass.  For our main menu we ordered the burger with sweet potato fries and the fennel sausage, pepper and onion pizza.  You will have to excuse the hamburger was ordered 'done' thus the appearance might suggest it was well but it was cooked and prepared exactly as ordered.  I would have ordered it medium but my guest had to have their meat well done.  The burger had tons of flavor and there was no mistaking - this was a very lean beef that had tons of flavor.  The garnishing was very fresh and flavorable and the bun was soft and fresh.  A little aioli on the side made a great pairing.   The pizza was the waiter‚Äôs third favorite choice on the menu, his first was the Flatbread Chicken Sandwich ‚Äì which we want to try when we return.  The pizza was excellent ‚Äì the peppers were yellow and red peppers and not the more bitter green peppers.  The sausage was loaded with flavor and every bite was pleasing to the palate.   It was large so I could only eat half of it after chowing down the starters.  With belly full and completely satisfied, I wanted to try out the cocktails at the bar and ordered a Bombay Sapphire tonic with a lime.   Again, like the wine we find that it was a good pour and came in a bucket‚Äì it was not to strong and not to weak ‚Äì it was poured just right.  Overall with the great food and drinks and a fantastic band made for the perfect evening out.
The Sideman music is inspired by 1970s Jazz/Funk/Fusion and influenced by artists like Tom Scott, the Crusaders, David Sanborn, and Larry Carlton.   We were especially happy and surprised when they played an Average White Band and Grover Washington, Jr. tune.  Welker put together group of top notch veteran and professional musicians that played with, and have experience in playing with, internationally known bands. So the entertainment that Red Brick pulled together was great.<//review><Rating>5</Rating>< gmapID>

< text>
I used to come to this restaurant before it changed ownership - and enjoyed it on those limited occasions that I could.  What I especially like about the current management is the option the feel more 'casual' when I come. I also appreciate a respectable menu of appetizers since I'm not often inclined to eat a full meal.
As before, the location is aces! It's one of the few scenic locations right on the river that has a photogenic view.
If anyone is open to recommendations, I would strongly suggest the fish tacos - WOW, I love them!</text>

I am normally pretty understanding when it comes to having to wait to get served but this place was ridiculous. It was not busy at all and our server Lacey disappeared for large quantities of time, nowhere to be seen in the restaurant; we had to request assistance from the hostess just to get our beverage order.  The food was okay, not nearly good enough to make up for the lousy service.  Additionally our bill was $105 (w/o tip) (2 glasses of wine each, crab cakes, he had steak, I had Cobb salad) and it took us two hours to finish the meal because of the bad service. I see no reason to go back, there are plenty of great places to eat in Petaluma.< /Text>

Good atmosphere for adults anf kids. Good menu selection (from pizza, fish & chips to ceviche and seafood pasta).
Had the fish tacos, ceviche and avocado & tuna poke, all were very good.
Right on the Peraluma river, great views.
Band was playing, but we got a corner table and wasn't too loud to talk with friends.
Service was great and our waiter was very helpful & friendly.
I think we got a great new place to go in town!!< /Text>

<user>106814983114996276857</user><Review>I've been coming to this Dim Sum place for awhile now! I come here if I want to sit down and enjoy dim sum at a restaurant. It's a great place for an early lunch IMO.

Food - I would kill for their fried shrimp balls. It's delicious. I have also tried their steamed shrimp dumpling, pork buns, shrimp rice noodle, shu mais, seasame balls, shrimp and chive dumplings, and much more. I recently tried their fish fried rice and their fried calamari which was also delicious - something I have ordered that wasn't the dumplings! I have some preferences for some dim sum but I mostly order the ones with the shrimp in it (if you can't tell already)! Their portions are very generous so this place gets you full easily! They have jasmine tea and oolong tea as options!

Service - The waitresses can be a little hard to communicate with because the restaurant can get busy! They give you a piece of paper and you mark how many of what you want, and they will bring it to you after. Some waitresses will try and serve you plates that you didn't order by walking around with trays of food or carts. DON'T GET HUSSLED! If you don't want it, don't order it! It's okay to say no. Some of the waitresses will also try to sell you on chicken or duck - again, DONT GET HUSSLED! Overall, from all my experiences they are friendly and will be prompt when asking for forks, refills for water or tea, and bringing extra napkins of that sort.

Environment - This place gets PACKED and LOUD! It's insane how busy this place gets. But that means this place gets good business. If you aren't used to eating at Chinese restaurants where everyone is talking or shouting across tables, or where you can hear a butcher chopping up meat for you or waitresses yelling orders across the restaurant. Then this place may not be for you.

Overall, I don't understand how this place has low reviews as it has not disappointed me yet. I hope it stays this way! I'll be back!<//Review><date>1559578431035</date>< name>
Mae-Elisa Schneider<//name>

King Kong Dim Sum is a good spot for some solid Dim Sum in San Leandro. That said, if you're not chinese/ can't speak chinese, you might want to find another spot to go to, as it's tough to navigate the fast paced world of dim sum here and you might in the sea of dim sum if you're lost in translation!

< Review>
Crissy Field is part of an urban national park, which, due to its location and scenic views, is popular with both locals, tourists, and dogs.

Crissy Field reopened in 2001. New and rebuilt sidewalks, boardwalks, and trails connect the field north to Fort Point, the Warming Hut (a cafe), and south to the Crissy Field Center, an environmental education center, and the Marina District. Since that time many buildings were restored and leased out as housing, office space, retail, and recreational facilities. The old temporary wood barracks were demolished and the grass airfield restored. Letterman Army Hospital, a large concrete structure, literally was ground to dust and the concrete recycled. In its place George Lucas relocated Industrial Light & Magic.</Review>
